Musow ka ca a la, u bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ kosɛbɛ, bawo u ye badenmusow ni denmusow ka denbaya ba ye.
Jatigiya sigilen bɛ cogo min na, o bɛ kɛ i n'a fɔ wuluwulu walima wulu kuluw, fɛnɲɛnɛma minnu man ɲɛnɛ ni waraba ye kosɛbɛ (nka u tɛ waraba gbakurun wɛrɛw ye) cogoya la, ani u bɛ mɔgɔ faga kosɛbɛ u ka sara kama fana.
Ɲɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛgɛnɛn A Maman yɛlenba, sigi da la, ka tɛmɛn walikɛ, ka yɔrɔ janba tɛgɛ, ani ka tɔgɔya ni fanga kanu, ni a bɛ se ka i to sɔgɔni fanga ka mara a ka ma.
Tigɛrɛ ye kelen ye ni jàtàw, silanfènèw, ani jagwarw ye bolokolonba kelen kɔnɔ (Genus Panthera). Jàniinɛ inani naani ninnu dɔrɔn de bɛ se ka kɔnɔbɔ.
Tigɛrɛ kununsi tɛ i ko lyɔn kununsi gɛlɛnɲuman de, nka a man diɲɛ kosɛbɛ i ko kuma murutilen minnu bɔra ni kanbele ye.
Oselo ye bagan fitininw dumuni kanu. Ni a be se, a be fenkɔɲɔnw, saanw, kuruɲɔgwɛnw ani kɔnɔnw minɛ. Bagan minnu oselo be taga a kan, u bɛɛ tara a ka dɔgɔ.
Karamɔgɔw miiriyɛ, jɔnmusow bɛ tɛmɛ ka nyɛnɛmaga tɔɲɔw ɲinini ka u dɔn ni u ninsɔndiyaba ye dugukolo kan, u bɛ u nɔfɛnw ɲinini.
U bɛ se ka ye koɲuman dibi kɔnɔ ni surukuɲɛɛ ye, ani u bɛ taama dogodogo fɛ fana kosɛbɛ. Waraba minnu bɛ farigan fɛ, olu bɛ u dɔnni sɔrɔ ni u yɛrɛ sɔgɔlen don u lamini na, o kɔfɛ u bɛ fanga don u kan.
Ni fɛnɲɛnama fitinin dɔ (jama fitinin dɔ) fara ka bɔ jama belebele la min bɔra a la (i n'a fɔ ni u yɛlɛmana kulu kan walima ba la, walima ni u yɛlɛmana gun kurunba dɔ kan walisa u kana se ka segin teliya la), u bɛna u yɛrɛ sɔrɔ yɛrɛsiyawuya wɛrɛ kɔnɔ a kɔrɔlen ka tɛmɛ minnu na u tun bɛ minnu na fɔlɔ.
Kɔrɔlenw bɛɛ jɛɲɔgɔn, sigida kura in bɛ nafolow ni ɲɛmɔgɔw sɔrɔ minnu tɛ kelen ye, o de la hadamaden kuraw bɛna ɲɛnajɛw walima dɛsɛw sɔrɔ minnu tɛ kelen ye walasa u ka se ka ɲɛmɔgɔya kɛ ni fanga ye ka tɛmɛ minnu kan u mako tun bɛ minnu na a fɔlɔ.
**Jamanakuntigiw sigilen tɛɛ minnu, olu ma yɛlɛma ka kɛɲɛ, u mago bɛ cɛɲiw kelen na i n'a fɔ a filɛ.**
Ni waati tɛmɛnen, k'a sababu kɛ jamana kura sigilenw bɛ ka ɲɛsin u sigiyɔrɔ kura ma, u bɛ daminɛ ka banɲɛn ka dɔgɔya ka tɛmɛ jamana wɛrɛw kan.
A laban, san waa lakawoliw walima miliyɔn caman kɔfɛ, jɛkulu fila bɛna cogoya caman sɔrɔ minnu bɛ danfara don u ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ fo u tɛ se ka wele ko suguya kelen.
An bɛ nin baarada in weele cɛsili, min kɔrɔ ye suguya kuraw dabɔri dɔrɔn de ye. Cɛsili ye kɔlɔsiyali ɲɛfɛ ye min tɛ se ka ban ani fɛnba ye ɲɛnɛma-ɲɛnabɔ kɔnɔ.
Binw bɛ oxygen da minnu adamadenw bɛ minnu nafi, ani u bɛ carbon-dioxide ta minnu adamadenw bɛ minnu bɔ.
Binw bɛ u ka dumuni da lamini na, tile fɛ fotɔsintezɛ jɛɛ̃ fɛ. U bɛ jigi di fana.
An bɛ an ka so jɔ yiriw la wa ani an bɛ faniw dilan yiriw la. Dumuni caman minnu an bɛ dumɛ, olu bɛɛ ye yiriw ye. Ni yiriw tɛ yen, fɛnɲɛnama si tɛ se ka ɲɛnamaya kɛ.
Mosasaurus tun ye a jamanakow la kongokoliba ye, o de kosɔn a tun tɛ siran foyi ɲɛ, fo mosasaurus wɛrɛw.
A da janya tun ye daɲɛgɛn 70 ni caman jɛgɛlen ye minnu tun bɛ jɛɲɔgɔnna, ani daɲɛgɛn sigilen wɛrɛ da kun na, min kɔrɔ ye ko fɛn si tun tɛ se ka bɔ a bolo min bɛ tɛmɛn a sira kan.

Filipinilu ka kɛlɛɲɛgɛn minnu Ameriki империализм kɛra, Filipinilu jɛɲɔgɔnw yɛrɛ de sara u gɔnɔ.
U.S. gouvɛrɛnaman ka koloniyali waati la, a tun ye wajibiyɔrɔw sigi u kan walasa ka taasiw sara walasa ka dɛmɛ don bɛɛnbaliyaw la ani faaɲɛw kan minnu bɔra Filipine gouvɛrɛnaman tɔgɔ la Wall Street bankiw sira kan.
Tiɲɛ na, Filipinikaw marayalen jatebaliya min sababu kɛra Filipinikaw tɔɲɔ na waati jan kɔnɔ, o bɛna Ameriki ka faamawuya ka nafɔba dɔnnenw sigi.
Templiers nɔnko faamuya kama, a ka kan ka waati min kɛlɛw ye a sigili sababu ye, o faamu.
Ɲɛnɛ minnu kɛra, o san kɛmɛlaw bɛ wele tuma caman na ko Ɛntɛrɛ-Aʒi, o ye Ɛriɔpu taariki ye san kɛmɛ 11nan, 12nan, ani 13nan (AD 1000–1300).
Àrabo tilelafɔlɔ kɔfɛ, ɲɛmɛɲɛmabɔ tilekɔrɔba sigira, wa a kɔfɛ, ɲɛmɛɲɛmabɔ tile laban sigira, min laban bɛ kɛ cogo la a bɛɛ ka kan ka a kan, san 1500 ɲɔgɔn.
Teknoloji ka jɛɲɔgɔnna ye kuma ye min bɛ miiriya gundo caman gundo jukɔrɔ, ka bɔ teknoloji-push walima teknoloji wajibiyaba la fo ka se miiriya sɛgɛsɛgɛlen ma ko hadamaden sɔrɔdasi bɛ tɛmɛ lɔgikifɛɛrɛ dɔ fɛ min bɛ sinsin saniyɛnsi sariya kan ani u yɛrɛ yira teknoloji kɔnɔ.
A lamɛnɛni jɛlen caman bɛ teknoloji ka jɔnjɔn ɲɛnabɔli kan, u bɛ hakili filanan dafa ɲɔgɔn na: ko teknoloji yɛrɛ ka bonya sigilen bɛ sira kan min tɛ tɛmɛ taamasiyɛn kan walima politiki ka seko kan, ani ko teknoloji ka "nɔ" bɛ jamana kan minnu bɛ yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya la, a tɛ jɛkuluw ka sigilen ye.
Misali la, mɔgɔ bɛ se ka a fɔ ko motɛri-gaari bɛ sira dafalen yiriwali ɲini o yɛrɛ la.
Nka, sira dɔgɔkunba dɔ sigicogo jamana bɛɛ kɔnɔ, a ma jɔɲɔ ɲɛnabɔ sɔrɔ farikolo la gɛlɛnw dɔrɔn kosɔn, o de la, baara kura cogoyaw bɛ sigi walasa ka gɛlɛn taamasiɲɛw dafalenya dɔgɔya.
Mɔ̌gɔ caman ka wotoro taa fɛ, o bɛ sira kan farati caman lase, min bɛ sababu kɛ furakɛli siraw kuraw sigili la walasa farikolo tiɲɛnenw ka ladamu.
Romantisismɛ tun bɛ ni dɛsɛ min bɔlen don diɲɛ kɛcogo gɛlɛn na, min bɔlen bɛ sɛbɛnnikɛlaw fɛ i n'a fɔ Goethe, Fichte, ani Schlegel.
Romantisismɛ kɔnɔ, dugukolo ɲɛnabɔli bɛ mɔgɔ kelen-kelen bɛɛ ɲɛnabɔ, waati tɛmɛni kɔ, a bɛɛ bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔsɔ ni dugukolo ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛ, ani a bɛɛ bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔsɔ ni dugukolo ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛ, ani a bɛɛ bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔsɔ ni dugukolo ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛ, ani a bɛɛ bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔsɔ ni dugukolo ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛ, ani a bɛɛ bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔsɔ ni dugukolo ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛ, ani a bɛɛ bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔsɔ ni dugukolo ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛ, ani a bɛɛ bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔsɔ ni dugukolo ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛ, ani a bɛɛ bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔsɔ ni dugukolo ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛ, ani a bɛɛ bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔsɔ ni dugukolo ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛ, ani a bɛɛ bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔsɔ ni dugukolo ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛ, ani a bɛɛ bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔsɔ ni dugukolo ɲ
Saaɲɔgɔn min na Pari ye dunya kurunba la lamɔgɔ faaba ye cogo min na, o cogo la Istambul tun bɛ jate Eropa ka masaya waati la lamɔgɔ faaba ye.
A ka caaya sababun ka a daminɛ cɛɲi kan san kɛmɛ naani kɔnɔ, ka tɛmɛ san kɛmɛ tan fɔlɔ la.
A ka caaya sababun ye ko Kurufera-mɔgɔw seginna ni tile-ɲumanw ni spice-ɲumanw ye minnu ka gɛlɛn ni Bizanzi marike minnu bɛ a yɛrɛ di.
O tuma le la faso moda kuntigiya yɛlɛman bɔnsɔn Konstantiniyye ka taga Pari.
Gothic sigili ɲɛtaa tɛmɛsira gɛlɛn tun bɛ san kɛmɛ tan ni san kɛmɛ tan ni kelen ni san kɛmɛ tan ni naani cɛ.
A dafɛn fɔlɔ la, donniyakow tun bɛ Bizɛnti taamasiyɛnw ta kosɛbɛ kɔrɔn fɛ.
Nka, komunikasiyon siraw dilanni kosɔn, tilebin fan fɛ mòdiw bɛ se ka tɛmɛ san 25 fo 30 kan.
Kɛ̀rɛnkɛrɛnba lajɛ, Ɛriɔpu tlebi fɔlila ka u yɛrɛ ka cogo dabɔ ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔnɔ. Wagati in ka bonya caman dɔ ye kɛlɛw sababu la mɔgɔw fɔlila ka tuɲuw dilanni ka finiw dafa.
Sɛnɛ min bɛ kɛ walasa ka dumuni hakɛ dɔrɔn sɔrɔ min bɛ sɛnɛkɛbaga ni a ka denbaya makɔnɔnko dafa, o ye sɛnɛ ye min tɛ tɛmɛn a yɛrɛ ɲɛfɛ.
Fɛnɲɛnajɛ bagan sɛnɛ ye cogoya nɔgɔn ye, a tɔgɔ ka ca a la, cogoya ɲuman, min bɛ kɛ ni bagan ji minɛn ye min bɔra yɔrɔjan mara la, a bɛ fara farafinna suguya caman kan walima cogoya nɔgɔn tɔw walasa ka bagan caman sɔrɔ.
Tarixɛ la, sɛnɛkɛla caman tun bɛ u yɛrɛ ka balo sɛnɛ de kɛ, wa o de bɛ ka tɛmɛ siɲɛ caman na jamana minnu bɛ ka yiriwa la.
Diɲɛnatigɛ minnu bɛ mɔgɔw lajɛn minnu hakili bɛ kelen, olu minnu ɲɛnɛmabɔra jamana ka cikanw fɛ ani k’u to u ka koo suguya dɔ sigi sen kan.
Lakolonw bɛ se ka jɛya a sababɛ ye kɔrɔ, siya, jamanakuntigiya, yɔrɔ, ani/walima cɛnimusoya sababu la.
Ɲɛnajɛ minnu bɛɛ bɛ se ka diɲɛsigida dɔ jɔnjɔnɛmaɲa yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya jira, olu bɛ se ka kɛ kumaɲɛnajɛ ye, ɲɛnajɛcogo ye, diɲɛnatigɛ ye, politikiko ye, jɛɲɔgɔnɲɛnajɛ ye, yɔrɔɲɛnajɛ ye, walima fɛnw caman jɛɲɔgɔnya ye.
Kulu dɔgɔmanw kɔnɔmɔgɔw ka ca a la ka taamasiyɛn di u ka kɛɲɛnɛ kan ni ɲɛjirali kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ni tagamasiyɛn ye cogoya la, minnu bɛ don jaatiraw, ɲɛnajɛ siratigɛw, ani kumaɲɔgɔnɲɛnɛw la.
Ɲɛjirali minnu bɛ kɛ cɛɲi walasa ka jɛkuluya ka nafa jira, o dɔ ye denmisɛnw ka ko gɛlɛnw jira minnu tɛ mɔgɔkɔrɔbaw ka jɛkuluya sɔrɔ ɲasiran, juguya, walima tɔɔrɔ kosɔn u lamɔni tuma.
O denmisɛnw bɛ wele ko "feral" walima sogo. Feral denmisɛnw dɔw bɛ mɔgɔw (ɲɛnajɛ u ka bangebaw yɛrɛ) dafalen, a kɛra ko o den tɔgɔ bɔli sababu kɛra bangebaw ka den hakili walima fɛɛrɛ tɔgɔlen gɛlɛn dafalen ye.
Denmisɛn minnu bɔlen tɛ mɔgɔ kɔrɔ, olu bɛ se ka denmisɛnya ɲɛnamaya gɛlɛn walima ɲɛnabɔ gɛlɛn sɔrɔ ka sɔrɔ u ka bila walima u ka boli.
A tɔw bɔra ko bɛgɛnw de ye u lamɔ; a dɔw fɔra ko u jɛgɛnw kɔnɔ u kelen kelen bɛɛ.
Ni denmisɛnba dɔ jɔn tɛ mɔgɔ ye ka a lamɔ, o denmisɛnba bɛɛ bɛ kɛɲɛ bɛɛ lajɛ, a bɛ kɛɲɛɲɛw jira (fɛɛrɛ minnu bɛ a fanga la), i n'a fɔ fɛn minnu bɛ o bagan minnu yɛrɛ ye, i n'a fɔ siran mɔgɔ ɲɛ walima a ma jati mɔgɔ ye.
K'à bò, gwàlɛgwàlɛ dàlajɛ kàn kà kàlanni yɛ̀lɛmà ani kà à diyà, jàtènɛ nìgɛ̀nnɔgɔ dìyɛ̀n bɛɛ bɛ taama tɛmɛ̀n ò kan.
Kalanfɛnw dilanni tɛ kalan sira ye, nka dɛmɛ ye min bɛ dɛmɛ di mɔgɔw ma minnu bɛ kalan kura dɔ kɛlaw la i n'a fɔ ɔridinatɛri porogaramu kura dɔ walima poroje kura dɔ daminɛ.
Dɛsɛbɔnw bɛ se ka kɛ lakana ni lakika ye, o kɔrɔ, karamɔgɔ ye dɛsɛbɔ ye, nka Microsoft Office kɔnɔ, pabilɔni fitinin sigiyɔrɔma fana ye o ye.
Ɲɛnajɛsɛbɛnw bɛ don porogaramu kɔnɔ ani u sigilen bɛ walasa ka ɲininkaliw kɛ, ka kunnafoni di, ani ka baara ɲɛfɔ minnu bɛ se ka gɛlɛn ka taamasiyɛn di kalanden ma a kelen na.
Denmisɛnw bɛ to baara ladon yɔrɔw la sababu caman kosɔn minnu bɛ taama ka bɔ janto tiɲɛni kan fo ka se tɔɔrɔ la, ani fanga gwaɲɛ.
Den misɛnni kelen tèna bonya yɛrɛ yɛrɛma jiriɲɔgɔn dafalanman, kanubagalanman ani karalanman kɔnɔ, nka u bɛ bonya o cogo la.
An bɛ miiri ko denbaya minnu bɛ denw ladon, olu bɛɛ ye sigida ɲuman ye denmisɛnnin ninnu ye.
An ka laadalikɛyɔrɔ dalajɛn bɛɛ ka kan ka sigiyɔrɔ ɲuman di, lakanaɲɛnuman tɔgɔbɔlenw, kalan gansan, ani kɛnɛya ladamuw.
Lakana waleya bɛ sigida ɲɛnama di min bɛ fɔlɔ fiyɛn ka bɔ yɛrɛ so kɔnɔ.
Internet ka dilan ani ka ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ ɲɔgɔn fɛ fɛnw bɛ jɛɲɔgɔn.
Internet sigiyaw yɛrɛ yɛrɛw bɛɛ sababu ye ka fara hakilina wɛrɛw kan baarakɛ ni dɛmɛ sɔrɔ cogo la.
Misali la, "kalanni" ni "ɲɔgɔn cɛɲi" dalajɛra i ko sababu kɔrɔw Internet sigiyɔrɔ la (James ni tɔɲɔgɔnw, 1995).
"ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya la" ani "ɲɔgɔn ka taamasiyɛnw tɛmɛnenw" fana bɔnna Eighmey ni McCord (1998) fɛ ka kɛ dɛmɛni kura ɲinini ye, u yɛrɛ ye mɔgɔw ka miiriya ɲinina kɔfɛ ɛntɛrinɛti dalajɛw kan.
Wideyo sɔrɔli baara kɛli ye kunnafoni kɔrɔlenw sɔrɔli yɛrɛmahɔrɔnyalenba sababu kɛ, ɲɛda ka yɛrɛmahɔrɔnyaw minnu bɛ kɛ milisekɔndi damadɔ kɔnɔ.
Ɲɛnɛmasɔrɔnman, a bɛ fɔ ko mɔgɔ bɛ se ka mɔgɔ nkalon faamu n'a ye ɲɛdafalen fitininw ɲɛfɔ tiɲɛ na.
Oliver Sacks, a ka a sɛbɛnni kɔnɔ min tɔgɔ ye ko "Président ka kuma," a y'a jira cogo min na mɔgɔw minnu tɛ se ka kuma faamu banakɔtaa kosɔn u bɛ se ka tiɲɛ dankɛ sirilenya kan jaati.
A ye seko minnu bɛ adamaden ka cogoya faamuya la, a bɛ a fɔ fana ko dumɛ bɛ se ka olu jɛnsɛn, i n'a bɛ cɛnw.
Ɲɛɲini minnu kɛra kɛmɛda XX kɔnɔ, olu jira ko gɛni yɛlɛma jɛɲɔgɔn fila de bɛ yen: minnu dogolen don ani minnu jiraalen don.
Jɛnɲɔgɔnkunnafoni kura bɛ fara gɛnɛtikisɛ cogoya kan, ani sugandili bɛ a bɔ cogoya min bɛ jira, o kɔnɔ.
Bolifɛnw faralen ni ɲɔgɔn kan ani ka tɛmɛsira kɛ, olu bɛ tɛmɛsiraw wuli ka taa ka segin bolow fila ni fila cɛ ni bɔnsɔn bɛɛ ye.
Dugu tigɛ kan, yɛrɛmahɔrɔnyalen min bɔɲɔgɔnɛ bɛɛ ka ca ni adamaden ta ye, a ka gɛlɛn a ma ka a ka amine-acide ɲɛnajɛw dafa yiriw la minnu bɛ sɔrɔ yen.
Ka fara o kan, ni o ma kɛ, a bɛ na ni gɛlɛyaw ye: jɛgɛlɛn bɛ kun, dumuni ɲuman tɛ sɔrɔ, a laban fana, saya.
Binjɛn yɛrɛfɛn minnu bɛ sɔrɔ teliya la kosɛbɛ, olu tun bɛna kɛ proteinɛ ye min bɛ bin-wolo ani bagan-bininw kɔnɔ, nka olu gɛlɛn don an ɲɔgɔn yɛrɛmafɛnw ma ka olu gbɛlɛya fo ni olu tosilen don.

Ni kow bɛɛ jate, an man kan ka kabakɔ, n'an bɛnbaw yɛrɛ ye u "faramuguba gɛlɛya" ɲɛnabɔ cogo kelen na min chimpanzéw bɛ savanna kan ka kɛ bi.
Sunɔgɔ bɔli ye waati ye min kɔnɔ i bɛ wuli i ka sunɔgɔ waati kɔnɔ ni miiriya ɲuman ye ka tila, ka sunɔgɔ tɛmɛnen kɔfɛ (miniti 10-60).
Nin bɛ se ka kɛ nɔgɔya la ni i ye waati-ɲɛnajɛ min bɔɲɔgɔn tɛ ka ca a kan, o baara kɛ walisa ka i kunbɛn ka i hakili sigi i fari la, i tɛ i wuli fɔlɔ-fɔlɔ.
Ni i y'i yɛrɛ sɔrɔ ka lɔgɔtɛri sɛgɛn i sugo la, a bɛ se ka bila yɔrɔ wɛrɛ la bon kɔkan, o bɛna i sinsin ka i wuli ka taa a faga.
Ɲɛnɛmafɛnw gɛlɛnyalen tɔ minnu sinsinnen bɛ farikolo laɲini kan, olu dɔw ye min jɔni caman min ye (kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la ji walima te, min bɛ dɔn ko a bɛ ji boliya), o bɛ mɔgɔ kɔnɔgbɔ, ka a blà a ka wuli ka sili boli.
Hɛrɛ min bɛ mɔgɔ dɔ bila a kɔnɔ, o bɛ bɛn ni fari ni hakili ɲagami hakɛ ye, nka a bɛ bɛn ka tɛmɛn.
Tando min ka dɔgɔ, hɛɛrɛ ni ɲɛnamaya gundo bɛ yen kosɛbɛ. Mɔgɔ kelen-kelen bɛɛ se ka lafiɲɛ ni nɛɛmɛ dafalen sɔrɔ.
Mɔgɔ bɛɛ se ka kunnafoni sɔrɔ. Fɛn kelen min bɛ i siɲɛ tɛmɛ, o ye an yɛrɛ ka gɛlɛyaw ni kojuguya ye.
Tibɛti Budayi sigilen bɛ Budaw ka kalan kan, nka a bonya ka ca ni Mahayana sira kan min bɛ kanuya jira, ani India Yoga ka cogoya caman fɛ.
Tiibɛti Budayi ɲɛnɛma la, a ka nɔgɔn kosɛbɛ. A sinsinni bɛ Koundalini Yoga, miiriyajateda ani kanuya gansan sira kan.
Kundalini Yoga kɔnɔ, Kundalini se (kunnafoni se) bɛ wuli yoga sigiyɔrɔw, niɲɛnajɛ sɛgɛsɛgɛliw, ɲininkaliw ani yɛlɛmaw fɛ.
Diɲɛ yɛrɛ yɛrɛw kunnafoni ni miiriyaw sababu la, fanga sababuw bɛ saniya, chakra-w bɛ labɛn ani kunnafoni hakili bɛ da.
Jamani tun ye juguya kelen ye J দ্বিতীয় জাতীয় জার্মানির সোয়ায়, কা কান মাকোন্কা গোন ই কায়ারা স. ইউ. এস. এ. নি এস. ও. কে সোয়ায়। জা য়ুরুগু বাইা কাবাতো কটা কুনকানিনিয়া তলাকাসিরা, ওয়ালিওয়া সিরা নি কালানকালানেকা গোন ই কায়ারা কা বাসিওয়া কা কুনওবোওরা ফালা।
Kɛlɛ kɔlɔwɔrɔ san fila kɔ, teriw bɛɛ tun bɛ ɲɔgɔn kan sisan, a Foyi Kɛlɛ daminɛna.
A tun ka kan ka taa ɲɛ san 40 nɔfɛn ani a bɛna kɛ ɲɛnajɛ tɛ, sɔrɔdasi minnu bɛ mɔgɔ wɛrɛw ka baarɛ kɛ, olu de bɛna a kɛ, kɛlɛ jɔyɔrɔw kan ka bɔ Afrika ka taa Azi, Afgaanistaan, Kiba ani yɔrɔ caman wɛrɛw la.

nɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛmaɲɛnɛ
O tuma kelen na, Zɛrman ka ji la kɛlɛjɛkulu, min bɛ U-boatw tigɛ kosɛbɛ, tun bɛ fɛn bɔɲɔw dilanni in bali ɲini.
Ni Alliés tun b'a daŋɛ, Ala ka ca a la, Alimaɲi tun bɛ se ka Angletɛri koɲɛ i n'a fɔ a koɲɛra Eropa fan bɛɛ cogo min na.
Ɲɛ̀gɛnw jirala ko u dàmɛnna fɔlɔ màссаɲɛ kɛmɛ tan ɲɔgɔn Zagros kuluw kan Iran jamana kɔnɔ.
Diɲɛkɔrɔlaw ni kabila damadɔw y'u mara walisa u ka sɔnɔ, u ka kunyi, u ka sogo, ani u ka fariw sɔrɔ nɔgɔn.
Fɛ̀nsɛnw màsàràw tùn bɛ́ mara jɛ́ɲɔgɔn na minnu bɛ́ taama kuluw kan walima dugu tɔ́w kan, bàmarala dɔ́w de tùn bɛ́ o màra, u tùn ye denmisɛnw walima kamɛlɛnw ye, i ko saga mara baganmɔgɔw minnu ka ca. O cogo mara ɲɛ̀naw bɛ́ baara la hali bi.

bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe bèe
Vatikan dugu mɔgɔ bɛɛ ye Roman Katoliki ye.
Hali k'a taa cɛmancɛma fɔlɔ fɔlɔw la, adamadennu tun b'a dɔn farikolo jɛlenw kan i n'a jɛlenw kan i n'a ye sanu, wari, ani kɔɔri, bawo olu bɛ se ka sɔrɔ siɲɛriɲɛ kan ka ɲɛsin olu ma ani u ka nɔgɔn ka boli ni minɛri minɛri tɔɔrɔw ye.
Aristote, hakilimalɔnba dɔ, a tun ye miiriya dɔ dilan ko fɛn bɛɛ jɛɲɔgɔn dɔ ye min dilannen walima fɛn naani dɔ walima u bɛɛ. U tun ye dugukolo, ji, fura, ani tasuma ye.
A tun bɛ i ko fɛnɲɛnɛma dalaw taani naani (ka bɔ a sigiyɔrɔ ɲɔgɔn na): gɛlɛn, jilen, gaz, ani plasima, hali ni a y'a miiri ko u bɛ tɛmɛ fɛnw kura kan ka kɛ minnu ye an bɛ minnu ye.
Alizee ye farankan ye minnu jikurun don walima farankan caman. Aw kana ɲinɛ ko farankan caman bɛ waati tigɛlen tabilon kan.
Aw ye fɛnɲɛnama caman i n'a ɲɔgɔn ye, kalisiyɔmu ani potasiyɔmu, olu jatebɔra misɛnw ye. Tiɲɛni tɛ, misɛn wɛrɛw fana bɛ yen i n'a ɲɔgɔn ye arizan ani sanu.
Aw bɛ se ka aliyasiw sɔrɔ minnu kɔnɔ, gɛlɛyawɛrɛ minnu tɛ bugɔw ye, i n'a fɔ karibɔni, olu man ca.
Duniya kɔnɔ fɛn o fɛn bɛɛ dilannen don farikolo la. Farikolo bɛɛ dilannen don yɛrɛma fitininw fɛ minnu tɔgɔ ye atɔmu.
Atɔmuw ka dɔgɔ kosɛbɛ fo ka se miliyaridiw bilibiliw bɛ se ka don dot min bɛ kuma laban na nin jɛlen in na.
O tuma, kalama ye teriw ye mɔgɔ caman fɛ a jiginni tuma.
Ayiwa, sɛbɛnni kura caman bɔlen kɔfɛ, nɛnɛbɔbɔn in ka caaya dɔgɔyara ani a baara fanan dɔgɔyara.
Bì mɔ̀gɔw bɛ sèbɛnw sɛ̀bɛ̀n kàrànfènnu kan bì, òlu tɛ jìrìbɔ̀lan sɔ̀rɔ̀ fo k’u kà ɲɔ̀gɔ̀n sɔ̀rɔ̀ abada.
Mɔgɔ bɛ se ka ɲininkali kɛ dɔrɔn walasa ka a faamu, klaviye ye na kɛ min ye ni fɛɛrɛ kuraw bɔra.
Atɔmɔbɔmbu bɛ baara kɛ ni sariɲɛ kan min b'a fɔ ko fanga ka kan ka kɛ walasa ka nɔgɔlen minnu bɛ proton ni neutron caman na, olu lajɛ ɲɔgɔn na.
A bɛ a n'i ko kɛrɛnkɛrɛnba dɔ min bɛ fanga caman di, o bɛ taama kulu kan. Ni i ye atɔmu gɛrɛgɛrɛn sɔrɔ ka fara a kan tɛmɛnen na, o bɛ fanga dɔw bɔ.
Atɔmu dɔw bɛ ni nukileyi jɛɲɔgɔnman tɛ minnu, o kɔrɔ ye ko u bɛɛ ka ca a la ka fara ɲɔgɔn kan ni nɔgɔya dɔɔnin ye walima nɔgɔya si tɛ.
Kalo dilancɛ sanfɛ ye kaburu ni binjɛ ye. Kalo dafalen kɔkan yɛrɛ ye minnu ye, o tɔgɔ ye ko dilanci.
Dugu golo ka caa ɲɛɛda fɛ kiilomɛtɛrɛ 70 ɲɔgɔn, a ka caa kiilomɛtɛrɛ 100 ɲɔgɔn dafɛ.
A bɛ nɔgɔn dɛgɛ minnu kɔnɔ, a bɛ gɛlɛn tɛmɛ minnu kɔnɔ.
A bɛ se ka mariyakɛ suguya caman bɔ tilebin fɛ, sabu golo man gɛlɛn. A yɛlɛmana yɛrɛmahɔrɔn ji ye ka yɛlɛn sanfɛ.
Kunnafoni kalanw bɛ sigi mɔgɔw bɛɛ ka miiriyaw walima minnu bɛ dɛsɛ u la ɲinini kan.
Ɲininkali innu bɛ a jira ko mɔgɔw ka makow ani/walima sɔnɲɛ minnu bɛ yen, olu donni bɛ mɔgɔw gundo la, k’a sababu kɛ u ka kɔrɔyaatɔbɔ ye.
Ɲininkali ninnu bɛɛ bɛɛ jɛɲɔgɔn kan ko mɔgɔ dɔw cogoya minnu b'a to u b'a fɛ u ka fɛɛn minnu sɔrɔ, ani fɛɛn minnu bɛ u lamini na minnu bɛna a to u ka fɛɛn dɔw kɛ walima u kana o kɛ.
Ɲɛnajɛko sɛbɛn kunnafoni dalajɛ ɲɛnabɔlaw ka caaman fila ye Maslow ka ɲɛnɛtakoɲɛnajɛ sɛbɛn dalajɛ ni Hertzberg ka sababu fila ka sɛbɛn dalajɛ ye.
A filɛ, mɔgɔw ka taamacogo fila bɛ se ka bɔ kun na managɛrw ye ka boli ka bɔɲɛ dɔgɔmanw ɲɛ, minnu tun ye uɲɔgɔnw ye. U kɔnɔ, kelen ye ka a janto a yɛrɛ la ko "cɛɲɛman kelen" (walima musow).
Ɲɛmɔgɔ sugu min bɛ nin ɲɔgɔnna, a ka gɛlɛn a ma miiriya minnu tɛ diɲɛ, olu ta, ka tɔnɔw lase mɔgɔw ma, ka baara ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛnabɔ, ka kunkanbaaraw di mɔgɔw ma, ani ka mɔgɔw jɔkun kan.
Ɲɛgɛnɛgɛn tɛmɛsiraw lajɛ, mɔgɔ kelen bɛ yɛlɛma fo a tɛ ɲɛnajɛ sɔrɔ, min bɛ miiri ko a ka kan ka kulu ka baara bɛɛ yɛlɛma ka a kɛ a yɛrɛ ta ye.
Ayiwa, kuntigi de ka kan ka kunnafoni di দল ka seko ani a tɔɔrɔ kama laban na.
Nin ko kɛta ka teli ka sababu kɛɲɛn kuntigiw ni sigilen tɔw cɛ.
Kulu masiriw bɛ taliɲuman dɔnnen kelen de kan i ko kulu kunnafoniw, nka danfara fitininw bɛ yen.
Ɲɔgɔnkunnafoni tigɛlenw ka mɔgɔw bɛ baara kɛ tuma caman na i n’a fɔ u sigiyɔrɔ yɛrɛ la, jɛkulu min bɛ yen, olu ka ladamuna ye.
U bèe ni hòrònɲasira gèlèn tè denbaya kònò bòlòfèrènw ye bawo u ka jèkulu bèe bè tali kὲ ni waati surunw ye minnu bè se ka sɔrɔ u ka yèrè-yèrè marayɔrɔw fɛ.
"Ɲɛnɛma tigitigi dɔ "ɲɛnɛma min tɛ yɛrɛ ye" (Larson ni LaFasto, 1989, p109) sɔrɔli, o fana ye jɛkulu jɛɲɔgɔn dɔ ye min tɛ yɛrɛ ye."
"Ɲɛnɛgɛn tɔn" ye ɲɛmɔgɔyaba ye minnu ma mɔgɔ kelen-kelen bɛɛ bɛ taariku. Ɲɛnɛgɛn tɔn bɛ sariyaw sigi mɔgɔ kelen-kelen bɛɛ ye.
Mun na jɛkulu bɛna a sɔn ka tɛmɛ waati gɛlɛn kan walasa ka kalan jɛkulu sigi sen kan? Kunnafoni kura bɛ jɛkulu ka kalan hakilina sigiyɔrɔ ye baara la taamasiyɛn dɔ ye.
Ni fanga bɛɛ minnu bɛ sɔrɔ, olu bɛ baara kɛ ni ɲɛnajɛ ye jɛkulu tɔgɔw la, danfɛn ni hakili dogoyalen bɛ se ka bɔ.
O kɔlɔjɛ, jɛkulu ka baara kɛɲɛfɔ ɲɔgɔn fɛ walasa ka gɛlɛyaw tiɛ, o bɛ se ka sababu kɛ walasa ka baara kura ɲuman dɔ sigi sen kan min bɛ miriya di sɛnɛkɛla sago ma.
Ɲɛ́fɔlɔ, ka sɔrɔ jɛkulu dɔ ka se ka kɛ̀ɲɛ, ɲɛmɔgɔya ka kan ka ɲɛnɛmali laadalakow da ani dɔnniya jɛlen ani jɛkulu ka kalan.
Angel (2006) b'a fɔ ko Continuum sira in ye sira ye min bɛ baara kɛ walasa ka dɛmɛ don jɛkuluw ma u ka se ka taama gɛlɛn kan.
Ɲɛnɛma-fanga-sɛnɛfɛnnu bɛ farankan minɛn ɲɛfɔlɔw jira min bɛ miiriya-taabolo dɛmɛ hakili ɲinini-siratigɛ la. O de kosɔn a bɛ ɲinini yɔrɔ masɔrɔ ani a bɛ a kɛ a ka ca a kan ko a bɛnnen.
Ɲɛnɛfɛnw ni jogoɲuman cɛ siratigɛ min bɛ mɔgɔ hakili la, o bɛ sayɛnsikɛlaw dɛmɛ u ka ɲininiw la.
A bɔ kabi waatijan, hakili tiɲɛni suguya caman, jugumanw, farikoloɲɛgɛnw ani muguwa bɛɛ bɛ nɔ bila jogo la ani k'hakili baara dɔw yɛlɛma.
Tekinoloji kura kunnafoni ka ca a sababu la an bɛ se ka hakili sigiyɔrɔw ni hakili ka baara ɲɛnabɔ cogo minnu ma ye fɔlɔ, an bɛ olu ye ani an bɛ ɲinini kɛ olu kan.
Nin bɛ kunnafoni ni fɛn caman di an ma walasa ka ɲɛjirali modɛliw jɔ minnu bɛ an dɛmɛ ka hakili cogoya faamu.
Hali ni AI tɔgɔ bɔra filimu fantasitiki la kosɛbɛ, AI ye ɲɛmɔgɔba ye komputɛri-sɛnsi ka yiriwali kɔnɔ, min bɛ tali kɛ taamacogo, kalan ani hakili sɛgɛsɛgɛli la masinɛ kɔnɔ.
Ɲininkaliw sɔrɔlɔgɔ kɔnɔ, fɛɛrɛw dilanni ɲɛsinin bɛ masinɛw ma walasa u ka baara minnu bɛ hakili gɛlɛn sɔrɔ, olu ka yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya kɛ.
Ɲɛɲɛjiɲɛw bɛ a la i n’a fɔ mara, labɛn ni waati dalajɛ, se ka jaabi di ɲɛnɛmɔgɔw ka bana sɛgɛsɛgɛli ni ɲininkaliw ma, ani fɔlɔ sɛbɛn sɛnɛ, kumakan ani ɲɛda.
Kow ni o kɛra kalankoɲɛw ye minnu bɛ taamasiyɛnw di ɲɛnako lakika ɲɛnabɔli kama.
Ɲɛnɛmabɔ-fɛnɛnnafɛnw labɛnnenw jɛnsɛnjɛnsɛn bɛ baara kɛ sisan jago, furakɛli, mekaniki ani kɛrɛkɛcɛɲɛw yɔrɔw la, i ko a jɔrɔlen cogo min na so kɔmputɛri ani tulonkɛminɛnw porogaramuw kɔnɔ.
Taama yɛrɛyɛrɛw ye kalanso sugu bɛɛ faanba ye. Tuma caman na, karamɔgɔ muso bɛna a ka kalandenw ta ka taga yɔrɔ minnu la basi taama tɛ se ka kɛ yɔrɔ minnu na.
Teknoloji bɛ furakɛli di ni ɲɛnajɛ taamasiyɛnw ye minnu bɛ kɛ internet kan. Kalandenw bɛ se ka musée ka fɛnw filɛ, ka jiwulansan sigiyɔrɔw taama, walima ka dɔnkilida lakika ɲumanw ye u sigilen tɛmɛ u kalasi kɔnɔ.
Sigilankan ka taama sanfɛ dɔ wɛrɛ fana ye sira ɲuman ye ka miiri taama kan ani ka kunnafoniw sigilan ɲɛnɛma kalanjɛw ye.
Ɲɛɲɔgɔn fɛ, san o san, Bennet kalan kɛɲɛgɛnw minnu bɔra Carolina Saheli, olu bɛ interneti wɛɛbisaite dɔ dilan u ka taama kan jamana faabaa la, san o san, wɛɛbisaite bɛ sɛnɛ, nka cogo kɔrɔw bɛ sigi interneti kan walasa u ka kɛ sɛbɛnnikɛyɔrɔ ye.
Blog-wɛrɛw bɛ se ka dɛmɛ k'a to kalannenw ka sɛbɛnniɲɛnɛmaɲɛ gɛlɛn ka ɲɛ. Hali ni kalannenw bɛ daminɛ tuma dɔw la u ka blog-ko kɔnɔ ni sɛbɛnnin gɛlɛn ani sɛbɛnniɲɛnɛmaɲɛ gɛlɛn, jama ɲɛsin bɛ yɛlɛma o ko ɲɛnama.
Kalandenw kɔrɔbɔli gɛlɛn ka ca tuma bɛɛ, blog sɛbɛnna bɛ taa a janto sɛbɛnni ɲɛnabɔli la walasa a kana kɔrɔbɔli sɔrɔ.
Blog lajɛlɛnw sɛbɛnni fana "bɛ kalandenw tilatilennin kɛ diɲɛ kɔnɔ." Mɔgɔw bɛ mun de ɲini walasa u ka ɲɛsigi o la, o bɛ kalandenw janto ani ka di (Toto, 2004).
Blogi ye baara ye min bɛ jɛkulu-ɲɔgɔnɛma dɛmɛ, ani a bɛ kalandenw jɔrɔ walasa u ka kalan faa ka tɛmɛ sikɔli tile kɔrɔbɔlen kan.
Blog "kɔrɔsigi ɲuman bɛ se ka kalandenw ka fanga jiidi u ka kɛ ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli ni miiriyajateda gɛlɛnw kɛ; internet fɛnɲɛnɛmaw jaabiɲɛnɛma tɛmɛsira fɛ, kalandenw bɛ se ka u ka yɔrɔw dafalen tɔw ka sɛbɛnninw kɔnɔ ani k’u yɛrɛ ka miiriya ɲɛnabɔ kɛɲɛɲɛninw kan (Oravec, 2002).

Sigisɛnɛgɛsigiw bɛɛ janto koɲuman ko gɛlɛyaw bɛɛ bɛ se ka sɔrɔ sigida minnu na, olu bɛ se ka taamasiɲɛw bɛɛ yɛlɛma.
Mɔgɔ min bɛ miiri ka taa jamana min na min bɛ se ka jati kɛlɛ yɔrɔ ye, o tigi ka kan ka kalanjɛ dɔnkilidaɲɛ sɔrɔ.
"Ni i ɲinina 'Hostile environment course' kan internet kan, a bɛ se ka kɛ ko i bɛ nafolo sɔrɔ yɔrɔ min bɛ dugu kɔnɔ."
Kalan in bɛna kunnafoniw bɛɛ minɛ minnu kofɔra yan, ni tilennenya gɛlɛnnen don kosɛbɛ, a tɛmɛnen don ni nɛnɛma kalan ye.
Kalan in ka ca a la, a bɛ kɛ tile 2 fo tile 5 cɛ, ani a bɛ sigicogo lajɛ, dɛmɛ fɔlɔ caman, ani tuma dɔw la, kɛlɛkɛnɛgɛw ka kalanni.
Gafe ni tilikalan minnu bɛ ɲɛnajɛ sigiyɔrɔ ɲɛnabɔli kɔnɔ, olu ka ca, nka sɛbɛnw minnu bɛ kɛlɛ yɔrɔw kɔnɔ, olu dɔgɔyara.
Taa tɛmɛsigiw minnu bɛ sɛgi-ka-bɔ a tɛmɛsigiw labɛn ka taa jamana wɛrɛw la, u ka kan ka u jɔnjɔnɲɛ minɛ ka ɲɛ, u ka segin-segin sɛbɛnw ka kan ka ɲɛ walasa u ka se ka segin.
Gwamnatiw ka sɔn ka pasepɔɔriw bɔ minnu jɛnsenni tɛ sɛbɛnnen (X) walima sɛbɛnw minnu labɛnnen don walasa u ka bɛn tɔgɔ ni jɛnsenni min bɛ bɔn, o cogoya bɛɛ tɛ kelen ye.
Gwamɛnti kɛnɛ kan ka sariya wara filɛnw bonya sago gɛlɛya ka ca ka cɛn.
Ɛɛnɛ siranfɛnw yɛrɛbɛn yɛrɛboli kɛlenw fana ka gɛlɛn kosɛbɛ san September tile 11, 2001 ɲɔgɔnna kɔ.
Ɲɛnɛjirali tɛmɛ siratigɛɲuman kan, mɔgɔ minnu yɛlɛmana ka bɔ u cɛɲiw ka na musow la walima musow ka na cɛɲiw la operasi ɲɛfɛ, olu man kan ka lamɛn ko u bɛna tɛmɛ jirikalanw fɛ ni u kunnafoni gundo ni u bonya sigilen tɛ.
Kɔgɔji-ji-bɔlɔnw ye ji min bɔra kɔgɔji dala, a bɛ segin ka taa sanfɛ, a ka ca a bɛ bɔ kɔgɔji-kɔnɔ-gɛlɛn wala min bɛ ɲɔgɔnna.
Ji gɛlɛya laɲiniw kosɔn, sɔgɔli bɛ jɛɲɔgɔn ka ca a bɛɛ la, a ka jan, ani ji jigin ka teliya bɛ se ka sigi yen.
Maa caman saya, olu ka tigɛ ka taama kuran ma, min bɛ se ka gɛlɛn.
Ni i bɔnna kulɛnti kɔnɔ, i ka segin ka tɛmɛ, o tɛ gɛlɛn ka tɛmɛ i ka sirilen kɛ cogo min na.
Ɲininkali kɛ yɔrɔ min ɲɛ, i tɛna minɛ yen tugun, walima a bɛ bɔ i ka seko kan ani ni i yɛrɛ ye jaabi sɔrɔ, a bɛ se ka kɛ i bɛ ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔn kunkanba kan.
**Kɔsegin-yɛlɛma-gasi ka gɛlɛn ka ca ni taama-yɛlɛma-gasi kan (ɲɛnajɛ waati man ca), a bɛ taa waatijan, ani a bɛ se ka gɛlɛn kosɔbɛ.**

ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛnɛma ɲɛn
Ni i seginna so ka bɔ jamana wɛrɛ la, i ye i jɔɲɔ ɲɛnɛma kura ma, ani i ka dɔnko dɔw tununna ka bɔ i ka so ta la.
Aw ye tɔ̀gɔya la tuma min na a fɔlɔ, a man kan ka kɛ ko mɔgɔw tun bɛ muɲu ani ka faamu, u bɛ dɔn ko lamɔgɔw jamana kura la, u mago bɛ ka yɛrɛ jɔ.
Maa si tɛ se ka miiri ko muɲu ni faamuyali fana kɛnɛn ka kan ka kɛ sigisɛgɛsigi tɛmɛsira ɲɛnɛmaw fɛ.
Ɲɛɲɔgɔ dafalen ni lamɛni fɔlɔ min bɛ piramidi kɔnɔ, o ye yɛrɛmahali ɲuman dɔ ye denmisɛnw fɛ yɔrɔ in kɔnɔ.
I bɛ se ka piramidiw ye dibi la ani i bɛ se ka u ye jɛɲɔgɔnya la fɔlɔ tulon ka daminɛ.
A teliya, tɔɲɔw ani jagokɛlaw ka kumaw bɛ mɛn tuma bɛɛ. Kumasiɲɛ ni jɛgɛlɛɲɛ taariku, a man diɲɛɲɛn ni kitabu ye.
Sifenksi sigilen don filiw la ka kɛ maana jan lakalikɛbaga ye.
Yɔrɔw bɛ jira piramidiw kan ani piramidi gɛlɛnw bɛ yeninɛ.
Shetland Saheliyan tilebiyanko minnu bangera san 1819, jamana caman ye hakɛ ɲininka a kan ani sigiyɔrɔ caman bɛ yen, ni ɲɔgɔn tɛmɛnen tan ni wɔɔrɔ minnu tun bɛ baara la san 2020.
Gunundu dalajɛ bɛ kilomɛtɛrɛ 120 ka jɛɲɔgɔn ɲɔgɔn taama tilebiran kɔrɔ. Min gɛlɛn ka tɛmɛn o bɛɛ kan, o ye Masa Jɔriji Gun ye, dugu min tɔgɔ ye ko Villa Las Estrellas.
Tɔn wɛ Livingston gun ani Deception yɛrɛ, yɔrɔ minnu na tasuma kurunba min bɔra tasuma kanfalen kan, min tɛ ban ka baara kɛ, o bɛ kuluba nafama di.
Ellsworth Dugukolo ye gunkan tilebiyanfan ye, Bellingshausen Ji dala a lamini.
Gundowole minnu be nin Dankan na, olu be fara ɲogon kan sanfɛkolo kan, o kɔfɛ u be wuli tugun ka Ellsworth Gundow kan 360 km jan sigi, Minnesota Ji kɔlɔn tɛmɛnen be a tɛmɛ.
Antarctica gɛrɛntaw lafiyalenw bɛɛ la gɛlɛnw bɛ dugu jɛlen kɔrɔnfɛ, minnu tɔgɔ ye ko Sentinel Range, Vinson Massif minnu san bɛ se mɛtɛrɛ 4892 ma, o tɔgɔ ye ko Mount Vinson.
Yɔrɔ janya-janyaw la, telefɔni-boli tɛmɛsiraw tɛ yen, sateliti telefɔni bɛ se ka kɛ i ka ɲɛnajɛ kelenpe ye.
Telefɔni sateliti tɛ telefɔni pòròtabili ɲɔgɔn ye kosɔn a tôro, bawo i man kan ka tô sôrô kan bolo sanfɛ walasa ka telefɔni wele.
Ɲɛnɛsirali kanjɛ fɔlɔn ye baarada caman de bolo, kuluba jɛɲɔgɔnw gansan, ani taamasiyɛnw minnu bɛ ni kunnafoni ni kumakan magow ye yɔrɔjan.
Aw ka telefooni baara dilanni yɛrɛ lajɛlen bɛ se ka kunnafoni caman di walasa ka don baara in kɔnɔ.
Gafe san kɔnɔ tɛmɛsira ɲuman dɔ min bɛ mɔgɔ caman diyɛ, o ye taama ni kalan ye.
Nin jiralen kosɛbɛ kalanni kɔfɛ, a b'u to ka san kelen ta sɔrɔ u ka taa lakɔli kɛ, ka a sɔrɔ u ka kalan tɛ nɔgɔya.
Ɲɛnajɛ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen caman na, ka tɔgɔ sɛbɛn sanɲɛmɛn-kalanjɛ kɔrɔsi la jamana wɛrɛ la, o bɛ se ka dɔ fara i ka seko kan ka don kalanjɛ gɛlɛn na i ka jamana kɔnɔ.
A tɔɲɔgɔn na, karamɔgɔ sɛbɛn ɲɛfɔli bɛna sara walasa ka sɛbɛn ɲɛfɔli kɛ nin kalanso kunnafoniw la.
Finlande ye kurun kɛlɛɲɔgɔn ɲuman ye. "Dala baa baa kelen" jamana in kɔnɔ, gun caman bɛ yen fana, dalaw ni dugu kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw kɔnɔ gɛrɛsyɛw la.
Gun kanw ni dala kɔnɔ, a tɛ wajibiya ka yati kɛ.
Hali n'a jɛlen kɔgɔjida gun lakolonw ani dankanba fɛnw ka bon kosɛbɛ jii taama kurunw bɛɛ ma, kurun fitininw walima gali fitinin bɛɛ fana bɛ se ka ɲɛnajɛ wɛrɛ di.
